 1403:        LOOP-BEGIN.                                                      00140400
 1404:            COMPUTE BINARY-CNTR-SAVE =                                   00140500
 1405:                ((PACK-CNTR + SUB1 + B) * (PACK-CNTR + SUB1 + A))        00140600
 1406:              + ((PACK-CNTR + SUB2 * B) * (PACK-CNTR + SUB2 * A))        00140700
 1407:              + ((PACK-CNTR + SUB3 * B) * (PACK-CNTR + SUB3 * A))        00140800
 1408:              + (SUB1 * A * SUB2 * B * SUB3 * C * SUB * D)               00140900
 1409:              + MASK3.                                                   00141000
 1410:            ADD BINARY-1 TO PACK-CNTR.                                   00141100
 1411:            ADD PACK1 TO MASK3.                                          00141200
 1412:            ADD PLUS1 TO FLAG1.                                          00141300
 1413:            IF PARM-MODE = 'DTE'                                         00141400
 1414:              CALL 'CAODSNAP'.                                           00141500
 1415:            IF MASK3 LESS THAN D                                         00141600
 1416:              AND CHECK1 LESS THAN CHECK5                                00141700
 1417:              AND BINARY-1 LESS THAN A                                   00141800
 1418:                ADD BINARY-CNTR-SAVE TO PACK-TOTAL                       00141900
 1419:                GO TO LOOP-BEGIN.                                        00142000
 1420:        SKIP1                                                            00142100
 1421:        END PROGRAM LOOP-COMPUTE.                                        00142200
